4/12/21 Note: this review is for the temporary covid vaccination site established at this location.
The vaccination site is very well organized with volunteers guiding candidates every step of the way. My appointment was at 10:45 and I was done with the shot at 10:53. You need to wait another 15 mins under observation for any reactions from the vaccine. There is a tent set up and seats are socially distanced for safety. Water bottles and candies are provided as well.
The site requires prior appointment and you need to have a consent form, a copy of a valid ID and your insurance.
This is a super smooth operation.</review>

It's a very nice, medium sized park. Long enough for walking the dog. Large dogs might need two laps. Very well shaded with lots of trees, 85% grass that is wonderful to lay down & relax on. Close to LongBeach airport as well.< /review>

< review>
While this facility was upgraded for the PanAm games I have never visited the site before as I am not into horse activities but I was invited by a friend to go on a bike ride on the Caledon trail and we ended up on a beautiful Sunday morning next to the Equestrian Park and we invited me to join him for breakfast and watch these beautiful horses go thru different jumping trials. First the park is massive in size, for car and trailer parking and for the facilities with many different rings for the competitive horses to do their thing. Second the concession stand makes a full breakfast, lunch and dinner!! Third the prices will very reasonable and the food was very good. We had choice of having breakfast inside or go outside and have a table and watch the horses and riders compete their tasks. I was 100% blown away by the facility the friendly staff, the fact we rode into the park on our mountain bikes, we were welcomed including having a nice bike stand to leave our bikes as we enjoyed breakfast. We go back many times as Caledon has this beautiful facility that nobody seems to know about unless you have a horse.<//review>

Camp Richardson Resort Beach is a beautiful public beach just north of The Beacon restaurant.  You can pay to park in Camp Richardson for $10, or hike in.

There's a reasonably priced watercraft rental facility so you can pedalboat, jet ski, etc.  On the beach there's also one volleyball court.

Great place, will definitely be back.<//text>
